{"answers": ["sperm", "sperm or egg cells", "ova"], "model_answer": "Haploid cells are not found in the human body. Haploid cells are typically found in gametes (sperm or egg cells) or in certain types of cancer cells, such as HAP1 cells. HAP1 cells are a type of near-haploid cell line that is used in biomedical and genetic research.\n\nIn the human body, most cells are diploid, meaning they have two sets of chromosomes, one inherited from each parent. {"answers": ["James Hutton", "geologist James Hutton", "William Whewell"], "model_answer": "According to the documents, the principle of uniformitarianism was introduced by William Whewell, a British naturalist, in the late 18th century. He coined the term \"uniformitarianism\" to describe the idea that the processes that shape the Earth's surface today are the same as those that shaped it in the past. This concept was later developed and popularized by Charles Lyell in his book \"Principles of Geology\" in 1830."}

{"answers": ["balance sheet", "The balance sheet"], "model_answer": "Based on the provided documents, the financial statement that involves all aspects of the accounting equation is the Balance Sheet.
